class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down size-3.5 text-fd-muted-foreground" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></button></div></div><p class="mb-2 text-lg text-fd-muted-foreground">Learn about the features available with GitHub Copilot and Prisma ORM, plus best practices and tips</p><div class="prose flex-1"><p>GitHub Copilot is an AI coding assistant that speeds up your Prisma ORM workflows, so you spend less time on boilerplate and more on data modeling, querying, and collaboration. With the GitHub Copilot extension in your editor, you can:</p>
<ul>
<li>Get Prisma-aware code suggestions as you edit your schema or invoke the client.</li>
<li>Chat with Copilot about modeling patterns, troubleshoot queries, or explore migration strategies.</li>
<li>Run common Prisma CLI commands (e.g. <code>prisma migrate dev</code>, <code>prisma db push</code>) via Copilot&#x27;s command-palette interface.</li>
<li>Scaffold Prisma schema models and generate Prisma Client code and run migrations directly from the Copilot chat interface.</li>
</ul>
<p>GitHub Copilot allows you to query the official docs via the <a href="https://github.com/apps/prisma-for-github-copilot" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank"><strong>Prisma for GitHub Copilot</strong> extension</a> and also perform automated <a href="/docs/guides/postgres/vscode#agent-mode">actions in VS Code agent mode</a>, such as scaffolding a Prisma schema, running seed scripts, and creating a production-ready Prisma Postgres database.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="query-prisma-docs-with-the-prisma-for-github-copilot-extension"><a data-card="" href="#query-prisma-docs-with-the-prisma-for-github-copilot-extension" class="peer">Query Prisma docs with the Prisma for GitHub Copilot extension</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The <a href="https://github.com/apps/prisma-for-github-copilot" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Prisma for GitHub Copilot extension</a> lets you fetch Prisma documentation directly in GitHub Copilot Chat. You can look up schema syntax, client methods, migration commands, and more from your editor.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="how-to-enable-the-extension"><a data-card="" href="#how-to-enable-the-extension" class="peer">How to enable the extension</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<ol>
<li>Install the <strong>Prisma for Copilot</strong> from the GitHub Marketplace.</li>
<li>Ensure <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/copilot/using-github-copilot/copilot-chat/asking-github-copilot-questions-in-your-ide" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">GitHub Copilot Chat is installed</a> and active in your code editor.</li>
<li>Open a file in your workspace and launch Copilot Chat.</li>
<li>In chat, prefix your question with the <code>@prisma-for-copilot</code> keyword:</li>
</ol>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span>@prisma-for-copilot How do I define a one-to-many relation?</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<ol>
<li>Install the <a href="https://github.com/apps/prisma-for-github-copilot" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Prisma for GitHub Copilot</a> extension.</li>
<li>Open your IDE.</li>
<li>Install the <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/copilot/managing-copilot/configure-personal-settings/installing-the-github-copilot-extension-in-your-environment" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">GitHub Copilot Chat extension</a>.</li>
<li>Open Copilot Chat and switch to <a href="https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/copilot/chat/chat-ask-mode" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank"><strong>Ask</strong> mode</a>.</li>
<li>Ask: &quot;<code>@prisma-for-github-copilot</code> How do I define a one-to-many relation?&quot; (If the <code>@prisma-for-github-copilot</code> namespace doesn&#x27;t show up after a few seconds, reload the chat.)</li>
<li>When prompted, authorize the Prisma app in your browser, then return to the chat.</li>
<li>After returning to the chat, resend the question.</li>
<li>Copilot returns the answer pulled straight from the Prisma docs.</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="use-github-copilots-agent-features"><a data-card="" href="#use-github-copilots-agent-features" class="peer">Use GitHub Copilot&#x27;s agent features</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>GitHub Copilot Chat offers an <strong>Agent</strong> mode in VS Code that can run Prisma commands. You can use the agent chat to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Run and inspect migrations.</li>
<li>Generate Prisma Client code.</li>
<li>Create a new Prisma Postgres database and update your <code>.env</code> file.</li>
</ul>
<p>You can type <code>Create a database named test-db and add its connection string to the .env file.</code> in the Copilot chat, and it will automatically create a new database named <code>test-db</code> and add the connection string to your <code>.env</code> file. To learn more about this, visit our <a href="/docs/guides/postgres/vscode#agent-mode">VS Code agent mode documentation</a>.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="customize-github-copilot-with-copilot-instructionsmd"><a data-card="" href="#customize-github-copilot-with-copilot-instructionsmd" class="peer">Customize GitHub Copilot with <code>copilot-instructions.md</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>You can tailor Copilot Chat&#x27;s behavior in your repository by <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/copilot/customizing-copilot/adding-repository-custom-instructions-for-github-copilot" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">adding a <code>.github/copilot-instructions.md</code> file</a>. This file injects your guidelines into every Copilot Chat session.</p>
<details><summary>Example <code>.github/copilot-instructions.md</code> for Prisma</summary><figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span># GitHub Copilot Instructions for Prisma Workspace</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>## General Guidelines</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>1. **Language**: English only.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>2. **Types**: Declare explicit types; avoid `any`.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>3. **Comments**: Use JSDoc for public methods and classes.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>4. **Exports**: One export per file.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>5. **Naming**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>   * **Classes/interfaces** → `PascalCase`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>   * **Variables/functions** → `camelCase`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>   * **Files/directories** → `kebab-case`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>   * **Constants** → `UPPERCASE`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>   * **Boolean flags** → verb-based (e.g., `isLoading`)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>## Prisma-Specific Guidelines</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 1. Data Modeling</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Domain-driven model names**: keep them singular (e.g. `User`, `OrderItem`).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Field naming**: use `camelCase` for fields (e.g. `createdAt`, `deletedAt`).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **IDs &amp; keys**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  model Post {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    id    Int    @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    uuid  String @unique @default(uuid())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Composite keys &amp; uniques**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@id([userId, role])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@unique([email, tenantId])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Enums &amp; constrained values**: leverage `enum` for fixed domains.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Soft deletes &amp; audit**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  model Base {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    createdAt DateTime @default(now())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    deletedAt DateTime?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 2. Indexing &amp; Constraints</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Single-column indexes** for frequent lookups:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@index([email])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Compound indexes** for multi-field filters/sorts:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@index([status, createdAt])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Full-text search** (Postgres-only):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  @@index([title, content], type: Brin)  // or Gin for JSONB</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 3. Migrations</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Descriptive names**: `npx prisma migrate dev --name add-order-totals`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Idempotent steps**: avoid imperative SQL in migrations.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Shadow database**: enable in CI to catch drift.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Never edit** migration SQL after it’s applied to any environment.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 4. Client Instantiation &amp; Connection Management</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Singleton pattern**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  // prisma.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  import { PrismaClient } from &#x27;../prisma/generated/client&#x27;;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  export const prisma = global.prisma || new PrismaClient();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== &#x27;production&#x27;) global.prisma = prisma;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 5. Transactions &amp; Batch Operations</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Multi-step atomicity**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  const result = await prisma.$transaction([</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    prisma.user.create({ data: { /*…*/ } }),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    prisma.order.create({ data: { /*…*/ } }),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ]);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Interactive transactions** for long-running flows.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Bulk writes**: chunk large inserts/updates to avoid timeouts.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 6. Precise Queries &amp; Performance</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Select only needed fields**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  await prisma.user.findUnique({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    where: { id },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    select: { id: true, email: true },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Avoid N+1**: use `include` or batch `findMany` with `where: { id: { in: [...] } }` or use database joins in prisma.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* Use **Cursor-based pagination**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 7. Raw Queries &amp; Client Extensions</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Raw SQL** when necessary, safely:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  const users = await prisma.$queryRaw`SELECT * FROM &quot;User&quot; WHERE email = ${email}`;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Sanitize inputs** with `Prisma.sql` for complex interpolations.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Client extensions**: use preview feature `clientExtensions` to add common helper methods.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 8. Error Handling</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Catch specific errors**:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  try {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    // …</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  } catch (e) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    if (e instanceof Prisma.PrismaClientKnownRequestError) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>      // P2002: Unique constraint</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Wrap in service-level errors** to add context before bubbling up.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 9. Testing</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **In-memory DB** (SQLite) or **Testcontainers** for integration tests.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Mock Prisma Client** for pure unit tests via `jest.mock()` or similar.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 10. Logging, Monitoring &amp; Metrics</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Enable query logging** in dev:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  new PrismaClient({ log: [&#x27;query&#x27;, &#x27;warn&#x27;, &#x27;error&#x27;] });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **APM integration** (Datadog, Sentry) – capture latency, errors.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 11. Security &amp; Best Practices</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Never expose** raw Prisma client in HTTP controllers—wrap in a service layer.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Validate inputs** (e.g. with Zod) before any DB operation.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Least privilege** DB users: use separate roles for migrations vs. runtime.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Rotate credentials** and load from secure vault (AWS Secrets Manager, etc.).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>### 12. Environment &amp; Configuration</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Centralize `DATABASE_URL`** and connection settings in `.env`.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Pin preview features** in `schema.prisma`:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>    previewFeatures = [&quot;clientExtensions&quot;, &quot;interactiveTransactions&quot;]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>  /```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>* **Version pinning**: match CLI and client versions in `package.json`.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure></details>
<p>Place this file at the root of your repository under <code>.github/</code>. Copilot Chat automatically applies these rules to every conversation in your project.</p></div><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4 border-t pt-6 text-sm"><a
